## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# TiDB SQL Privilege Check and RBAC Enforcement Audit

## Your Task

Audit the privilege and RBAC enforcement in pingcap/tidb. Find all Go source files under pkg/privilege/ and pkg/planner/ that implement privilege checking for SQL statements. Identify: the PrivilegeManager interface, the MySQLPrivilege cache, the RequestVerification method and its callers, the role graph resolution logic, and any files that map SQL statement types to required privileges. For each file report the path and its role in the privilege check flow.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/tidb--v8.5.0.

512026-03-08T19:53:34.104721agentmessage-
I am thinking...: Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the privilege and RBAC enforcement in TiDB. Let me compile all the findings:

## Files in pkg/privilege/

1. **pkg/privilege/privilege.go** - Defines the `Manager` interface (PrivilegeManager interface) with all privilege-checking methods including `RequestVerification`, `RequestDynamicVerification`, `ActiveRoles`, `FindEdge`, `GetAllRoles`, etc.

2. **pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go** - Defines the `AuthConn` interface used during connection authentication.

3. **pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go** - Implements the `Manager` interface via `UserPrivileges` struct. Contains `RequestVerification`, `RequestDynamicVerification`, `RequestVerificationWithUser`, `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege`, `DBIsVisible`, `ShowGrants`, `ActiveRoles`, `FindEdge`, `GetDefaultRoles`, `GetAllRoles`, `IsDynamicPrivilege`, `RegisterDynamicPrivilege`, `GetDynamicPrivileges`, `ConnectionVerification`, etc.

4. **pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go** - Contains `MySQLPrivilege` (the in-memory cache of MySQL privilege tables), `Handle` (thread-safe wrapper), `roleGraphEdgesTable` (role graph), `FindAllRole` (BFS role graph traversal), `FindRole`, `RequestVerification` (core privilege check logic), `RequestDynamicVerification`, `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege`, `LoadAll`, `LoadRoleGraph`, `LoadUserTable`, `LoadDBTable`, `LoadTablesPrivTable`, `LoadColumnsPrivTable`, `LoadDefaultRoles`, `LoadGlobalPrivTable`, `LoadGlobalGrantsTable`, `DBIsVisible`, `showGrants`, etc.

552026-03-08T19:55:44.363405agentmessage-
Here is the complete audit of privilege and RBAC enforcement in TiDB v8.5.0:

---

## Privilege and RBAC Enforcement in TiDB v8.5.0

### 1. `PrivilegeManager` Interface

**File:** `pkg/privilege/privilege.go`

The `Manager` interface (aliased as `PrivilegeManager` in some contexts) declares all privilege-checking operations:

| Method | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `RequestVerification(activeRoles, db, table, col, priv)` | Static MySQL-style privilege check at global/db/table/column scope |
| `RequestVerificationWithUser(db, table, col, priv, user)` | Same but for a specific user identity (used for view definer checks) |
| `RequestDynamicVerification(activeRoles, privName, grantable)` | Dynamic privilege check (BACKUP_ADMIN, ROLE_ADMIN, etc.) |
| `RequestDynamicVerificationWithUser(privName, grantable, user)` | Dynamic check for a specific user |
| `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege(activeRoles, privName, grantable)` | Dynamic check **without** SUPER fallback |
| `ActiveRoles`, `FindEdge`, `GetDefaultRoles`, `GetAllRoles` | Role management |
| `ConnectionVerification`, `DBIsVisible`, `ShowGrants` | Connection and visibility |

`GetPrivilegeManager(ctx)` / `BindPrivilegeManager(ctx, pc)` bind/retrieve the Manager from the session context.

---

### 2. `MySQLPrivilege` Cache

**File:** `pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go`

`MySQLPrivilege` is the in-memory snapshot of all MySQL privilege tables. It has two layers:
- **`immutable`** — slices of `UserRecord`, `dbRecord`, `tablesPrivRecord`, `columnsPrivRecord`, `globalPrivRecord`, `dynamicPrivRecord`, and `roleGraph map[string]roleGraphEdgesTable`
- **`extended`** — hash maps (`UserMap`, `DBMap`, `TablesPrivMap`, `Dynamic`) for O(1) lookups

The **`Handle`** struct wraps `MySQLPrivilege` with an `atomic.Pointer[MySQLPrivilege]` 
... (truncated)

Calls `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` to get all effective roles (user + active roles, filtered by actual grants)\\n2. Checks global user privileges (`matchUser` \u2192 `UserRecord.Privileges`)\\n3. adding:\\n- SEM (Security Enhanced Mode) checks for invisible tables/schemas\\n- Extension access check functions\\n- Auth plugin verification hook\\n\\nCallers of `RequestVerification` in `pkg/planner/`:\\n- `pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go`: `CheckPrivilege` iterates `visitInfo` and calls `pm.RequestVerification` for each static privilege entry\\n- `pkg/planner/core/preprocess.go`: direct call during preprocessing for table access checks\\n- `pkg/planner/core/point_get_plan.go`: `checkFastPlanPrivilege` for point-get fast path\\n- `pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go`: direct call for view definer privilege checks (`RequestVerificationWithUser`)\\n- `pkg/planner/optimize.go`: calls `CheckPrivilege` after building the logical plan\\n- `pkg/planner/core/plan_cache.go`: calls `CheckPrivilege` for cached prepared statements\\n\\n### Role Graph Resolution Logic\\n\\nIn `pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go`:\\n- `roleGraphEdgesTable` is a map `roleList map[string]*auth.RoleIdentity` representing edges in the role graph (which roles are granted to a user/role)\\n- `decodeRoleEdgesTable` populates `roleGraph` from `mysql.role_edges` rows: for each `(FROM_USER, FROM_HOST) -> (TO_USER, TO_HOST)` edge, it records that `TO_USER@TO_HOST` has been granted role `FROM_USER@FROM_HOST`\\n- `FindAllRole(activeRoles)` performs a **breadth-first search** (BFS) over the role graph starting from the active roles, collecting all transitively granted roles\\n- `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles(user, host, activeRoles)` first filters `activeRoles` to only those actually granted to the user (via `FindRole`), then calls `FindAllRole` for BFS traversal\\n- `FindRole(user, host, role)` checks if a specific role is directly granted to a user by looking up `roleGraph[user@host].Find(role.Username, role.Hostname)`\\n\\n### Files Mapping SQL Statement Types to Required Privileges\\n\\n**`pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go`** is the primary file mapping SQL statements to privileges:\\n- `visitInfo` struct (line 81): holds `privilege mysql.PrivilegeType`, `db`, `table`, `column`, `err`, `dynamicPrivs`, `dynamicWithGrant`\\n-
